  gif            Returns the First Found Image on Google Images for this Input

  pokedex

  pokebattle     Fights a Pokemon Boss
  pokeboss       Displays Boss Info
  pokehelp       Pokemon Battle Sim Help
  types          
  level          Displays your Current Information
  lookup         Displays your Current Information
MusicPlayer:
  youtube        Adds a Song for the Bot to Play
  songs          Prints the songs in the queue
  loop           Plays the current song again
  playlist       Adds songs from a predefined playlist to the songs list
  skip           Skips the Current song
  search         Searches for a song
  music          Returns the current status of the Music Bot
  extendplaylist Extends a custom playlist
  song           Returns information about the current playing song
  Radio          Toggles Radio Mode
  viewplaylist   Views the songs of a playlists
  desc           Decription of the Current playing song

18 Jan 2017 07:43:45 : LimitlessMc, private, Botfuzzy77#2209, Welcome to the Pokemon Battle Sim!
Here you fight together against Pokemon Bosses. There are 4 areas, 'Easy', 'Medium', 'Hard' and 'Insane'.
To fight a boss, you use the command `;pokebattle`, along with the area you wish to fight in, and a set of moves you will fight the boss with.
An example of this is the following:
`;pokebattle easy ngfse` 
which means you will be fighting the easy boss with battle combo of Normal, Grass, Fire, Steel, and Electric.
You can use any combination of the 10 moves which can be found on ';types'

Here you fight together against Pokemon Bosses. There are 4 areas, 'Easy', 'Medium', 'Hard' and 'Insane'.
To fight a boss, you use the command `;pokebattle`, along with the area you wish to fight in, and a set of moves you will fight the boss with.
An example of this is the following:
`;pokebattle easy ngfse` 
which means you will be fighting the easy boss with battle combo of Normal, Grass, Fire, Steel, and Electric.
You can use any combination of the 10 moves which can be found on ';types'
